[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue is a heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability with a scariness score of [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcategorized as a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte-read-heap-buffer-overflow. The vulnerability occurs when [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe JSON parser attempts to read [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte at memory address `[0m[1;36m0x5020000000b5[0m[39m`, which [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0x5020000000b5[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Stack Trace Analysis:**[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe error occurs in the following call chain:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. `json_parse_ex` at `[0m[35m/src/shadowsocks/src/[0m[95mjson.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m620:29[0m[39m` - This is where the [0m     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. `json_parse` at `[0m[35m/src/shadowsocks/src/[0m[95mjson.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m958:11[0m[39m` - The public API function [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation, resulting in the overflow.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe heap-buffer-overflow occurs at line [0m[1;36m620[0m[39m in `[0m[35m/src/shadowsocks/src/[0m[95mjson.c[0m[39m` during[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing of the JSON literal value [0m[32m"false"[0m[39m. The vulnerability is caused by an [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moff-by-one error in the boundary check at line [0m[1;36m618[0m[39m.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Detailed Mechanism:**[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWhen the parser encounters [0m[32m'f'[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe start of [0m[32m"false"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, it performs the following [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moperations:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Line [0m[1;36m618[0m[39m: Checks `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` to ensure sufficient bytes remain[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Lines [0m[1;36m618[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m620[0m[39m: Pre-increments `state.ptr` and reads [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m more characters [0m[1;39m([0m[32m'a'[0m[39m, [0m[32m'l'[0m[39m,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m's'[0m[39m, [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**The Bug:** [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The check verifies only [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes are available, but the parser needs to read [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtotal positions: the current [0m[32m'f'[0m[39m plus [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m more characters[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- With a [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte input [0m[32m"fals"[0m[39m: `[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m4[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` evaluates to `false`, allowing [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexecution to proceed[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The parser reads positions [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[32m'f'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[32m'a'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[32m'l'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[32m's'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, then attempts to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mread position [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Position [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m equals `end`, causing a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte read beyond the allocated buffer [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboundary[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Similar Vulnerabilities:**[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
